<script type="text/javascript">
   var side_bar_html = "";
   var gmarkers      = [];
   var map           = null;
// A function to create the marker and set up the event window function
   function createMarker(latlng, name, html, imagem ) {
      var contentString = html;

//ATENÇÃO ERLON: Ja esta ok!!! MarkerImage(url:string, size?:Size, origin?:Point, anchor?:Point, scaledSize?:Size) Erlon essa é a disposição dos elementos do MarkerImage
      var icones = new google.maps.MarkerImage(imagem,
          new google.maps.Size(20,34),
          new google.maps.Point(0,0),
          new google.maps.Point(0,17),
          new google.maps.Size(10,17));
      var marker = new google.maps.Marker({
          position: latlng,
          map     : map,
          icon    : icones,
          title   : name,
          zIndex  : Math.round(latlng.lat()*-100000)<<5
      });


      google.maps.event.addListener(marker, 'click', function() {
        infowindow.setContent(contentString);
        infowindow.open(map,marker);
      });
// save the info we need to use later for the side_bar
      gmarkers.push(marker);
// add a line to the side_bar html
      side_bar_html += '<a href="javascript:myclick(' + (gmarkers.length-1) + ')">' + name + '<\/a><br>';
   }
// This function picks up the click and opens the corresponding info window
   function myclick(i) {
      google.maps.event.trigger(gmarkers[i], "click");
   }

   function initialize() {
// create the map
      var myOptions = {
          zoom: 4,
          center: new google.maps.LatLng(-14.7166, -55.8666),
          mapTypeControl: true,
          mapTypeControlOptions: {style: google.maps.MapTypeControlStyle.DROPDOWN_MENU},
          navigationControl: true,
          mapTypeId: google.maps.MapTypeId.ROADMAP
      }

      map = new google.maps.Map(document.getElementById("map_canvas"), myOptions);

      google.maps.event.addListener(map, 'click', function() {
         infowindow.close();
      });
